In general, the hardware of the hotel is indeed limited, but the service is indeed in place, and the price of more than 400 is worth it, and I should come again.

msg:#Hotel leads the way# Miyun Ruiheim, 22 years of Dragon Boat Festival
On the evening of May 28, the epidemic press conference announced that hotels and homestays in Beijing suburbs were lifted. I immediately went online, but most of the homestays were not online yet. After chatting with a few, the boss just got the news, and the price was raised during the communication process. Still worried about the repeated policy, I booked Huairou Thai Lotus Court first (cancellation free of charge). On the 2nd, the Huairou policy "does not accept guests from Haidian Fengtai". After canceling it, I changed the reservation to Miyun Ruihaim. Yuan.
